);

CREATE SEQUENCE STR_SQ
INCREMENT BY 1
START WITH 1
NOMAXVALUE
NOCACHE
NOCYCLE;



CREATE TABLE STORE (
STR_NO VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
STR_NAME VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
STR_COU VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
STR_CITY VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
STR_ADDR VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
STR_TEL VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
STR_ATN VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
STR_PRE NUMBER(2,0) DEFAULT 30,
STR_SHIP VARCHAR2(5) DEFAULT 'TRUE',
STOCA_NO VARCHAR2(15),
STR_ACC VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
STR_PAS VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
STR_IMG BLOB,
STR_STAT VARCHAR2(15) DEFAULT '«Ø¸m¤¤',
STR_MA VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
STR_REP NUMBER(1,0) DEFAULT 0,
STR_LONG NUMBER(10,7),
STR_LAT NUMBER(10,7),
STR_NOTE CLOB,
CONSTRAINT STORE_STR_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY (STR_NO),
CONSTRAINT STORE_STR_NAME_UK UNIQUE (STR_NAME),
CONSTRAINT STORE_STR_ACC_UK UNIQUE (STR_ACC),
CONSTRAINT STORE_STOCA_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY (STOCA_NO) REFERENCES STORECATEGORY (STOCA_NO),
CONSTRAINT STORE_STR_PRE_CK CHECK(STR_PRE BETWEEN 5 AND 90)
);

CREATE TABLE DISH (

);

CREATE SEQUENCE MEM_SQ
INCREMENT BY 1
START WITH 1
NOMAXVALUE
NOCACHE
NOCYCLE;

CREATE TABLE MEMBER
(MEM_NO VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
 MEM_ACC VARCHAR2(16) NOT NULL,
 MEM_PW VARCHAR2(16) NOT NULL,
 MEM_NAME VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
 MEM_PHO VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
 MEM_MAIL VARCHAR2(60) NOT NULL,
 MEM_VIO NUMBER(3) DEFAULT 0,
 MEM_STAS VARCHAR2(10) DEFAULT '¥¿±`',
 MEM_IMG BLOB,
 CONSTRAINT MEMBER_MEM_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY (MEM_NO),
 CONSTRAINT MEMBER_MEM_ACC_UK UNIQUE (MEM_ACC));

(MEM_NO VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
 STR_NO VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT FAVORITE_MEM_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY (MEM_NO) REFERENCES MEMBER (MEM_NO),
 CONSTRAINT FAVORITE_STR_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY (STR_NO) REFERENCES STORE (STR_NO),
 CONSTRAINT FAVORITE_FAV_PK PRIMARY KEY (STR_NO,MEM_NO));

INCREMENT BY 1
START WITH 1
NOMAXVALUE
NOCACHE
NOCYCLE;

CREATE TABLE ORD
(ORD_NO VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
 MEM_NO VARCHAR2(15),
 STR_NO VARCHAR2(15),
 ORD_EV NUMBER(3),
 ORD_TYPE VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
 ORD_PRI NUMBER(9,2) NOT NULL,
 ORD_DATE DATE NOT NULL,
 ORD_STAT VARCHAR2(15) DEFAULT '¥¼½T»{',
 ORD_EVA CLOB, 
 ORD_ADD VARCHAR2(65) ,
 CONSTRAINT ORDER_ORD_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY (ORD_NO),
 CONSTRAINT ORDER_STR_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY (STR_NO) REFERENCES STORE (STR_NO),
 CONSTRAINT ORDER_MEM_NO_FK FOREIGN KEY (MEM_NO) REFERENCES MEMBER (MEM_NO));

INCREMENT BY 1
START WITH 1
NOMAXVALUE 
NOCACHE
NOCYCLE;

CREATE TABLE ADMINISTRATOR
(ADM_NO VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
 ADM_ACC VARCHAR2(16) NOT NULL,
 ADM_PAS VARCHAR2(16) NOT NULL,
 ADM_NAME VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
 ADM_ADRS VARCHAR2(65),
 ADM_PHO VARCHAR2(35),
 ADM_POS VARCHAR2(35),
 ADM_MAIL VARCHAR2(65),
 CONSTRAINT ADMINISTRATOR_ADM_NO_PK PRIMARY KEY (ADM_NO),
